The result of monitoring and assessment of the present state of atmopharic environ-
ment is shown in Table 9-2, 9-3 and 9-4. The assessment results show, that Sulphuric
dioxide pollution in Jincheng Mill and the surrounding atmospheric environment is not se-
rious, the average pollution index value in a day is 0. 04-0. 20, the maximum pollution
index at one time is 0. 009-  0. 52. Nitrogen oxide density at monitoring points is low.
The total suspension particle pollution is obvious, the average pollution index in a day is
0. 6-7. 57, manimum pollution index at one time is 0. 24-5-. 25, the average excess
standard rate in a dry reaches 90%/, excess standard points are numerous and it is the
principal polluting matter in atmospheric environment of the said area. Its source not only
comes from Mill production, but also from the dust in the main comunication lines. Both
the combined pollution index (Table 9-5) computation and the classification of atmo-
spheric environment quality (Table 9-6) show, a single T. S. P would put the atmospher-
ic quality of the said area into a warning state, into a leveL of intermediate pnllution.

fore in the construction process various pollution matters polluting the atmosphere wiLl be
produced, besides, the vehicles and machinery in construction will raise considerable
dust. Sand and stones laid in open areas, and the dug-out earth and stones will also raise
dust under the action of the wind. The pollution matter on atmosphere wlU posibly be
S02,NO., CO, dust etc.
Due to te lack of materials about the construction process, the present assessment
on the impact on atmOspheric environment during constuncion process is madc in only
qualitative description terms.
The construction area in pollution treatment of Jincheng Paper Mill is confined with-
in the boundaries of the old mill, during construction process, the pollution matters on at-
mosphere are.drained off disorderly, the principal pollution matters are S0, CO released
by transportation vehicles, and dust raisd by them, as well as the combustion gas pro-
duced by construction machinery. The above-said pollution matters are produced in con-
struction process in qeurral. Since the construction takes place inside the boundaries of the
mill,it will not yield impact on outside atmophere.
The construction in the water supplies project includes the foundation structures,
well-drilling and digging and laying of water network pipelines, the construction is con-
fined to points and lines, all of them are situated in open-air agricultural areas, there-
fore, the construction process is considered to yield certain impact on the surrounding at-
mospheric envirorment but not very serious.
9. 1. 4. 2   Analysis of the impact of the construction  project on atmospheric
environment
The statistical materials of wind speed, wind-direction frequency for five continuous
years provided by local neteorological station and a pollution coefficient in a certain di-
recon defined as the ratio of a wind-direction frequency in certain direction to the wind
speed of tat direcion, are used to describe the paible degree of poUution in the down-
stream wind direction, the statistical results are shown in Table 9-5. lag 9-5 sham'
that the still-wind frequency is 15. 2 Y%, the dominant wind direction is SSW, the direc-
tion second to the dominant one is NNW and N. The statistical result of pollution coeffi-
cient frequency also reflects the fact that, the pollution coefficients in the dominant wind
103



direction and in the direction second to the dominant one are much higher than those in
other directions. The rose chart of wind direction in that area and rose chart of pollution
coefficients are shown in Fig 9-2.
The drainage of atmospheric pollution matters in the project is characterised by the
fact that, the charcoal stoves work all the year round, while the coal-burning boilers of
the watcr distribution plant only work for warmth during winters and the coal burning is
relatively slight, therefore, in the atmospheric poUution diffusion computation only the
naximum falling to ground pollution density and its corresponding distance are consid-
ered, and a computation model from the GB3840-83 "Technical Principles and Method
for Formulating Drainage Standards in Local Atmospheric Pollution Matters" is selected.
The 30-minute maximum ground density in down stream wind direction of an isolated
srnoke funnel is computed by the following formula:

a2

wind speed into the formules for maxnmum falling to ground density C.. and the corre-
sponding distance X,.. to get the maximum value among all density values, we get the ab-

9. 1. 5 Suggestions on Control Measures in Atnuspheric Pollution
There are three principal atmospheric pollution sources in the water source removal
and reconstruction project and the Jincheng Paper Mill curbing poUution treatment pro-
ject. In the water source project two coal-burning boilers are added, in the curbing pollu-
tion water treatment project a charcoal stove for producing artificial charcoals is added. In
accordance with related regulations the boilers are selected from finalized products suiting
the atmospheric protection requirement, the installed dust remover should meet the re-
quirement on boiler smoke drainage as set down in the DB91-GO--89 "Drainage Standard
on Polluted Water and Waste Gas of Liaoning Province". In boiler operation, manage-
ment should be strengthened, the dust removing facilities should work normally. The
charcoal stove is a thermo-mechanical facilities which carbonizes the carbon-containing
grasses and wooden materials to produce carbon raterials with a high heat value, the car-
bonizing process is a process that makes the mnaterial to volatilise combustible organic mat-
ters in a certain temperature in a reduced environment ( inadequate oxygen ) and dry-
distill a large amount of carbon. Therefore, this prooess requires that the waste gas
drainage is completed wholly by natural draft of the smoke funnel. Considering the great
amount of waste gas, the stress of preventing atmospheric poUution should be laid on rais-
ing the height of the smoke funnel under the condition that charcoal stove operation is not
affected, so that -smoke and gas can diffuse into a higher space.

sites are lacking, the impact of it is not considered in the present assement, but we think
it will not exert a great impact in noise to the surrounding environment.
9. 2. 5 Nolse Prevention Measures
T he project noise mainly comes from the machinery of the pumping station and the
pumping room of the water distribution plant. To prevent noise, in treating noise source
on the one hand, low-noise facilities should be used, shock-reduction cushion on large
machinery foundation should be laid, stretching/contracting joins for shock reduction
should be installed in water pump entrance and exit, in the doors and windows of duty-
rooms double-window panes should be installed for sound insulation. In treating noise
propagation on the other hand. planting broadleaf arbor trees inside and outside the
pumping station and water distribution plant walls should be considesed in order to make a
sound insulation screen.
During the construction process, when the transportation cars run through the popu-
lated areas, the speed should be lowered and sirening should be prohibited to reduce imn-
pact of communication noise on the population as far as poesible.

10. 1. 1 Analysis of the Impact of the Water Source Removal and Reconstruction Pro-
ject on the Economic Development and the Living Quality of the People In
Jlnzhou City
The present water-supply system of Jinzhou is already far from meeting the require-
ments,especially as the economy develops and the people's living standard rises, the re-
quired amount of city water rapidly increases,so the water source removal and recon-
struction project becomes more and more urgent, it affects the economic development and
the raising of living standard in Jinzhou city.
The present state and prediction of water usage,water drainage and industrial output
of the exploited area and the urban area of Jinzhou are shown in Table 10-1.
As seen from the table,the quantity of water used by the industry is 161,O000m' per
day,the industrial output is 4,950,000,000 yuan. According to the prediction,in 1995.
the water used by the industry will increase to 247,000 m' per day,the industrial output
will increase to 6,540,000,003 yuan, water used by the industry will increase
86, DOOm3 every day. If living water is added .it is predicted that the water deficit per day
will reach 98,900m'.
If new water source is not constructed in Jinzhou before 1995, and besides,the wa-
ter source is more polluted, a serious water deficit will come about, which certainly will
affect the industrial development. Some new and big industrial projects will not be able to
start due to the restiection caused by the water deficit. Thus the economnic development of
Jinzhou will be restrained, and the strategic plan of economic development of Jinzhou in
1995 will be hard to realize.
Ihe water source removal and reconstruction project is very important as viewed
from the rising living standard of the people. The present state and predietion of living
water usage in the urban area and exploited area is shown in Table 10-2.
From the table it is seen,the average amount of water used per day per man 162
litres in 1990. In 1995,the predicted average amount of water used per day per man will
reach 180 litres,the population will also raise from 569,000 in 1990 to 629,000. Rapid
increase of living water usage require the construction of new water source and the raising

10. 1. 2  Analysis of the Impact of WatCr Source Removal and Reconstruction Project on
Employment Problem
After putting into production in 1995, the water source removal and reconstruction
project not only will promote economic development and the rising living standard, but
will also provide to the society more employment opportunities.
After putting into production ,i, will add 87 employees.among them 9 are adminis-
trative personnel, 51 are pumping station employees, 36 are Damu Water Distribution
Plant employees.
The social benefit brought by the water source removal and reconstruction project is
enormous. Especially after its putting into production, broad employment opportunities for
the society will be brovght about due to the rapid development of industry.
The calculated industrial output after its putting into ptoduction basing on the num-
ber of employees and workers and the labour productivity of 1990 shows that in 1995 ,the
number of employees and workers in the urban area of Jinzhou will reach 453,200 ,an
increase of 110,000 in comparison to that of 1990. Considering the progress of science
and technology, up to 1995, the employees and workers will increase at least 55,000 due
to the direct and indirect impact of the project and the average increase of employees and
workers is over 10,000 every year,so that rate of unemployment will decrease obvious-
ly. In general,the project will directly or indirectly provide more employment opportuni-
ties for the citizens of 3   .z.ah_
1. 3  The Impact of Water Source Project on The Dminage
Load of Jinzhou City and the Measures



10. 1. 3. 1 The impact of the water source project on drainage system of Jinzhou City
and the corresponding measures.
After putting into production in 1995, the water source project will greatly increase
the load of the Jinzhou drainage system. At present ,there exist serious problems in the ur-
ban area drainage systeni, water-logging appears when torrential rain comes. The stan-
dard of the city's trunk canals is low,the drainage capacity is small, water-collecting fe-
cilities are distributed irrationally ,and the draining capability is poor. Now the municipal
government is reconstructing the drainage network,and the reconstruction network will be
completed before 1995,which will increase the drainage system capacity.
A prediction is mnade in the amount of industrial water in use and the amount of wa-
ter drained in Jinzhou urban area on the 1990 basis with due consideration to structural
adjustment of industrial products ,technological reform and technical progres factors. The
predicted results are shown in Tables 10-S3 and 10-4.
From the tables it is seen that in 1990 the drainage of industrial water in Jinzh  ur-
ban area per day is 136,900m3,the total drainage is 218,000m3 per day . It is predicted
that in 1995 drainage of industrial water is 210.000m3 per day,the total drainage is
289,839ms per day,therefore,in 1995 the amount of drainage will increace 71,839ms
per day. In the table the predicted drainage of the two pollution exits,Houwuli and Chang-
tunhe,is smaller than the present drainage, this is caused by the combined effect of prod-
uct structural adjustment and technological reform in the nearby factories.
The plan of drainage and pollution water treatment of Jinzhou Cty is shown in the
attached figure.
At present the drainage network of Jinzhou can only reach drainage capacity stan-
dard of p= 0. 25'-0. 5 year, therefore, for the drainage capacity to reach a standard of
P= 1-2 year to meet the requirement in water source removal and reconstrucion project
and the sudden torrential rain draining,two projects,the. building of stop-flow ditch in
Renmin Street and reconstruction of covered ditch in Shiyin Street,will be conducted,the
total funding for the projects is 9,010,000 yuan RMB.
After its putting into production in 1995,the urban area will be divided into Shiyin
drainage area(Shizhen west eXit), Renrin drainage area (Qunyi exit) ,Weidong drainage

The project funding is 30,000,000 yuan,it can receive the pollution water drained

Xiaolinghet,including pollution water of Xiaobagou.

tion water from Xizhenxi exit to Jinfang exit is transported bv a stop-flow ditch to the
said field for treatment.

the downstream section of Xiaolinghe, and the said polluted water treated . The project
funding is 17, 000, 000 yuan.

tons per day ,they will treat the polution water from the city area ,besides an oxidizing
pond with a volume of 1, 000, OOO9m in the downstream is added for a further treatment,
so the river water of Xiaolinghe will reach the GB 3838-88 i standard.

10.1. 4  Anmlyus and Objt of Impact of the Used Land of the Water Source Projet
The used land of the water source project includes the land used for water-fetching,
pumping station and transportation pipelines, water distribution plant and water distribu-
tion pipes. The pumping station occupies 2. 2 hectares of land and is situaed in thz north
side of the Baduandongbu village road(farmnand) ,the transportation pipeline does not run
through the village and needs no removal of residences. The water distribution plant will
be built in the north side of Damu distribution plant, the construction occupies 2. 2
hectares of land.
The perranently requisitioned land of the pumping station and water distribution
plant will change the purpose of land use permanently, causing a minor change in the e-
cological environment of the surrounding area. For example,the plantation area will de-
crease, noise influerce of plant will ernerge,the resting ground for wild animals and in-
sects will decrease.
The construction of the transportation pipeline will change the earth layers ,the earth
fertility will decrease,the cultural produce of the next year will be affected. At the same
time,the construction will affect the tillage of cultures.
In sum,the land used for water source project will exert a negative influence on sur-
rounding environment,affecting the economnic benefit of the nearly farmers, therefore,
during the project a certain fund will be used for compensation,at the same time,af-
forestation will be conducted in the two requisitioned areas to reduce environmental ef-
fects and to gradually recover agricultural production along the transportation pipeline
area. Expenses for various land usage are shown in Table 10-8.

10. 2 Social Impact Assessment of Water Pollution Treatment of Jinchen_L
Paper Mill
10. 2. 1 Assessmrnent Analysis of the Secondary Pollution Caused by the Use of Glutinous
Agent
To protect the water source of Daling Rirer ,the waste water drained from production
in the present project iS to be used in a eombined way. Ir pulp making a multi-section re-
verse washing by double- network pulp- washing machine will replace the present pulp-
*   washing method by washing pond. In the recorery of thick red liquid for producing gluti-
nous agent, it is planned to produce 50.000 tons of glutinous agent yearly.
The glutinous agent produced in the pollution water treatment project of Jincheng
Mill is mainly sold to the zinc production plant,etc in lluludao for nodulizing iron ores.
The glutinous agent contains a certain quantity of sulpnuric salts like magnesium disul-
phate, Hydrogen disulphate etc. These salts enter the furnace with ore nodules for baking
and smelting, in the process of smelting and burning a certain quantity of S02 gas in pro-
duced; accounting for a yearly production of 150,00; tons of glutinous agent, and a
recorery of 2,178. 38 ton/d of thick red liquid,the burning process of glutinous agent
will produce 6. 97 ton/d of SOz. (SOz is accounted to be 0. 32 % of the thick red liquid),
i.e. 2,544t/d.
2,178. 38X0. 32%=6. 97t/d,or 2.5-1-4t/a
When the glutinous agent is used in zinc plant (byproduct sulphuric acid), the
SO2 produced in the baking proces and that produced in the baking process of fine zinc
ores will be used to produce sulphuric acid.so it will not yield secondary pollution.
129



When the gultinous agent is used in plants not adopting recovery of SO2, the plan;,
should increase S02 treating facilities, otherwise secondary pollution will take place.
10. 2. 2- The Impact of the Treatment Project on Natural lAndscape of Daling River
Although Daling River is a river with a foul water ,the landsepae in arews beyond
Jincheng is not disagreeable. When the pollution water from Jincheng Mill enters, due to
the great amount of suspension particles,reed crumbs and the blackish waste water that
nmixes. into the river,the surface of the river is spread with reed crumbs, fluffy matters,
the color of the river water becomes mixed in black and yellow,causing a very disagree-
able appearance. On the left side of river beach,the pollution drainage canal of Jincheng
Mill Shed an odous from suspension particles and the residual S02,it is nauseating espe-
cially in the rainy hot weather.
After the start of the treatment project ,on the surface of Daling River there are no
more crumbs,the suspending flaffy matter in river water becomes slight with the recovery
of filres,and the water colour approaches that of upstream, the odous of the beach also
greatly disappear. In gereral,after the start of the project,the landscape of Daling River
greatly improves.
10. 2. 3  Analysis of Impact of the Treatment Project on Employment Problem
After the start of the treatrnent project, Daling River pollution is not only alleviated
and certain economic benefit created ;the employment problem of personnel is also solved.
For full utilization of production waste water, four workshops are to be built in
Jincheng Mill: workshop for recovery of thick red liquid; workshop for glutinous agent;
workshop for recovery of white water and workshop for artificial charcoal. An increase
of 150 people for employment. So after the start of the treatment employment problem for
153 people will be solved, which alleviates the pressure of social labour force.

Source Project
The impact of the project on the society, economy and environment is broad. Table
11-1 gives an environmental impact matrix of the project. In the matrix, the upper right
of diagonal represents the level of environmental impact.the positive and negative signs
represent positive and negative impact respectively, the number represents the grade of im-
pact, 4 indicates "very big" .3-"Relatively big", 2-"normal", 1-"slight". The lower part
of the matrix represents the kind of "impact" ,ST-short term,LT-long term,R-reversible,
IR-irreversible, L-small scope, W-big scope ,and A-negligible.
The positive impact of the water source project on social economy and environment
is very great, the main aspects are supply of unpolluteddrinking water to the city people,
so their health will not be harmed by water pollution,provision of potential or direct eco-
nomic and social benefits,such as the supply of water resources by the new water source
to economic and social development, provision of employment opportunities directly or
indirectly to the people,etc. After putting into production of the project.it brings a nega-
tive impact on ground surface water and underground water. Palliating measures should
be adopted to the above negative impacts. It should be noted also,that due to the supply
increase the water load and pollution load of the city's drainage system will increase, cor-
responding plan and adjustment measures should be adopted to prevent the emergence of a
series of new environmental problems.

coal burning boiler and the noise of pumping station will exert certain influence on the
surrounding water and atmospheric environment and environmental noise. But the above
said pollution rmatter produced bv this proe.s is verv small.and it is far away from the

11. 2. 2 Asessmcnt of Economic Benefits
Through the measures of technological reform reequipment, closed-cricuit circula-
tion and combined utilization etc. , the pollution water treatment.project of Jincheng Mill
changes harm into henefit, changes wastes into values, and fundamentally controls the
drainage of poUution water and th' principal pollution matters of the mill.
'he project will produce glutinous agent 150, 000 tons, artificial charcoal 4,000
tons yearLy; recover paper- making white water 10,200, 000 tons, paper pulp fibre
4,600 tons. and talcum powder 8,000 tons yearly. The economic benifit is impressive.
The analysis of various economic indicators is shown in Table 11-11.
As seen from the table, the scope of the project is big, funding is great, in a certain
period after its putting into production, the loans from domestic and foreign countries
must be repaid, a temporary econmic burden will be laid on the mill. As the loans are
gradually repaid, its econornic benefit emerges more and more. After normal aperation,
the project will gain a profit of 7,751,000 yuan yearly, the period of fund recovery is
15 years

EnviriornenLil mnanagement is a measune to solve environmental problems. and to
coordinate the relation between social economic development and the environment. The
following management rules are put forward basing on the characteristics of the water
source removal and reconstruction project and Jincheng Paper Mill pollution water treat-
ment project.
Conmmunication management rules during construction
Many transportation vehicles are used during the construction of the two projects,
the vehicle sirens must be strictly controlled. Night traffic is prohibited. The vehicle noise
should be reduced to a mimnimum.
Asphall innapcnent rules during contruction:
Asphalt is used in great quantities during construction, it sheds harmful gas and
smoke when heated. therefore the use of asphalt should be strictly coiitrolled, the heating
position should be selected rationallu to bring the least harm to the population.
Boiler management rules
Adhering to the principle of the "three simultaneities" in the project construction and
enviroment facility, the boilers built in the water so irce project must be equipped with
suitable equipment for elimination of smoke and dust, the height of smoke funnel must
meet the requirements. The normal operation of smoke and dust elimination equipment
must be guaranteed.
Management rules for Chloride workshop and the use of Chlorine gas
The training of personnel on the post of Chloride gas employment must be strength-
ened, those not qualified must not be allowed to attend. There should be strict prevention
measures against leak of Chlorine gas. The safetv of working personnel must be ensured.
there should be warning equipment and method of elimination leaks.
Training rules
I o raise the level of environmental management and vocational standard of environ-
mental protection, thd working personnel must be trained regularly, the sense of environ-
mental safetv must be raised. The personnel conducting environmental monitoring must
participate in a regular quality check, to ensure the reliability of monitored data.
Management rules for the I three simultaneities" of environmental protection of the
recvctea DaDer                                           i.m.   i . rns gn irnnn  -,



project
The control of fund usage during the "three simultaneities" construction period of
environmental protection must be strengthened. Work must be checked. At least one
check every month, the records must be closely examined, probliems encountered in the
checks must be reported in time and corrected in time.
Management rules of environment in construction sites
Tne surrounding environrment of the construction sites must be protected during con-
struction to prevent the damage to natural environment, prevent and alleviate the pollu-
tion of dust, pollution water, wastes, noise, shock, etc of construction to the surround-
ings and population areas. Before completion of the construction the damages caused to
the environment during construction must be repaired and recovered.
Environmental monitoring and reporting rules In project operation period
To ensure the quality of the new water source, not only strict environmental moni-
toring rules are needed besides, if pollution accident appears or extraordinary condition
emerges, timely report must be made to the responsible departments to adopt effective mea-
sures.
The construction of the water source project lays a burden to the task of externel en-
vironmental monitoring, special duty monitoring personnel must be added.
In the Jincheng Mill treatment.project additional monitoring personnel must be added
to the original staffing of the monitoring station.
12. 2 The Monitoring System and the Content of Monitoring
The positioning of monitoring points is an importart link in monitoring, the opsitions
of monitoring points is directly related to the amount of information of the invirornment
quality and the accuracy of the information. The determination of monitoring points re-
flects the environmental quality in the two projects. In accordance with this it is suggested
to establish. The monitoring points in the following areas.
12. 2. 1  Mlonitoring Points and Systems of the Water Source Project
On the rightside shore of Zhaojiawopu section is Dalinghe establish three observation
145



wellsof 20m, 40m, 65m depth (1,2.3 of Fig 12-1 ) to continuously monitor the
change of water quality of the underground water-supply. If abnoimality is discovered,
report in due time. This monitoring will be carried out by environmental department of
1iZe project.
12. 2. 2  Monitoring Points and System of the Jincheng PoUution Water Treatmcnt Pro-
12. 2. 2. 1 Monitoring of pollution drainage exit
Monitoring points are established in Jincheng Mill pollution drainage ditch exit (4 of
Fig 12-1), (The pollution water ditch under the bridge). Routine check wiU be done ev-
eryday. A continuous monitor will be conducted every season, the sampling interval is 2
hours. It should be well arrange in accordance with labour and equipment, for a eontinu-
ous moritoring of 24 hours. The task will be earried out by Jincheng Paper Mill.
12.2.2. 2  Dalinghe monitoring
Routine monitoring points (6 of Fig 12-1) will be established in Zhaojiawopu, to
conduct monitoring during dry, medium and full water periods. It is suggested that the
task be carried out by municipal environmental moritoring department.
12. 2. 2. 3 A monitoring point will be established in the pollution drainage ditch at
Thaojiawopu (5 of Fig 12-1). 3-5 sampling points may be established according to the
width of the river. At least 5 sampling should be made in one monitoring. The task wil
be carried out by Jincheng Paper Mill. The positions of the above-said points are shown
in Fig 12-1.
12. 2. 3 Items of Monitoring
The water source project is used for supplying living water to the people, so the reg-
ular items of tap water must be monitored, at the same time, it is necessary to monitor
the waste water pollution drained by Jincheng Mill treatment project, the items for moni-
toring are CODw,CODo, oils, phenols. The monitored itemns of Jincheng treatmnent pro-
ject are COD,,, CODa oils, phenols, pH, quanitity of blow.

13 MEASURES ADOPTED FOR POLLEMION TREATMENT
UNDER EXTRAORDTNARY CIRUMSTANCES AND SUGGES-
TIONS
13. 1 Accidental Drainage from Jincheng Pollution Water Treatment Pro-
ject and the Adopted Measures
13. 1. 1 AccIdenlal Drainage of Pulp-naking Thick Red Liquids and the Measures for
Treatment
The main content of treating the pulp-making waste liquid is to recover the thick red
liquid to produce glutinous agent. According to the engineering analysis, after completion
of the pulp-making waste liquid treatment project, the total amount of thick red, liquid
treated per day is 2,178. 38 tons, the design adopts an imnported spray-film vacuum e-
vaporator. Since the maintenance requirement for the evaporator is hign, the condition of
thich red liquid evaporation process is poor, if due to some cause the evaporator stopc or
works abnormally, the thick red liquid may be drained off without treatment, the great
148
recycled oaoer                                         eI.r. lsifniflfl.



amount of pollution matters thus drained will cause serious pollution accident.
In accordance with the practical circumstances of the plant, it is impossible to add a
standby evaporation facility, so the following measures are suggested.
13. 1. 1. 1 In order to prevent a short-term accidental drainage of thick red liquid, it is
suggested to add a thick red liquid storage pond for accident. The effective volume of the
pond should not be smaller than that for a drainage amount of 12 hours . V/hen tempo-
rary accident occurs in the production of glutinous agent, the thick red liquid is poured n-
to the accident pond, and be treated after production returns to normal.
13. 1. 1. 2 If the glutinous agent can not be recovered after 12 hours, the whole pro-
duction work of the pulp-making workshop should be stopped.
13. 1. 2 Abnormal Drainage of Artificial Charcoal Project and Recovery of White Water
and the Suggesions for Treatment
For recovery of white water in the present project a slant-plate sinker is used. Since
the treatment technology is simple, if nanagement is strcnthened and the operation rules
a: seriously observed, there should not be serious accidents.
If trouble occurs in the reed-crumb recovery equipment of charcoal production, it
will cause an accidental drainage containing dust and reed curmbs, therefore, on the basis
of strengthening the management of reed-crumb recovery equipment, paralel standby e-
quipment should be added, storage volume should be increased so as to prevent accidental
drainage.
13. 2    The Possible Emergence of Accidental Drainage from  Chlorine
Adding Process in the Water Source Poroject Water Distribution
Field ana its Treatment Measures
The newly-built Danmu Water Distribution Plant in water source project consumes
100kg/d of sterilised Chlorine gas, normally, 4. 17 kg of Chlorine gas is added per hour.
149



In normal circumstances, a tiny amount of leakage is allowable in the Chlorine equip-
ment, for the Chlorine shop a forced ventilation is employed, and since the leakage is ex-
tremely slight, in normal circumstances the tiny amount of Chlorine in the drained atmo-
sphere should not caus obvious effect to the environment.
The Chlorine adding equipment operates continuously for long periods, and if the
operation and naintenance of the equipment is incorrect, accidental leakage of the equip-
ment will emerge, and if it is not discovered and corrected in time, a large amount of
Chlorine gas will be drained into the atmosphere, shedding influence on the atmspheric
enviroment and causing serious pollution accident.
In accordance with the Chlarine technology, the following measure are suggested.
13. 2. 1 In order to discover Chlorine gas leakage timely, and control the anount of
leakage to a minimal scope, Chlorine leakage warning measures in the Chlorine
ps storage of Chlorine workshop should be adopted.
13. 2. 2 All-enclosed forced ventlation should be instaled In Chlosrine workshop to en-
sure that all the leaked Chlorine gas enters Chlorine gps treatment equipment
through wind- induction system, to prevent an uncontrollable area source
drainage.
13. 2. 3  Adopt a highly effective treatment of absorption of Chlorine gas by lkali, to
- ensure an effective treatment of high density Chlorine gas of accidental
drainae, and ensure a drainage after reaching the standard.
14 CONCLUSIONS AND SUGGESTIONS
14. 1 The deposited fan areas of Dalinghe and Xiaolinghe of Jinzhou con-
tain abundant underground water resources. The underground water
of the said area is not only the whole water supply source of Jinzhou
urban area, but also one of the water sources for Panjin and Jinxi
150
rescycId DaDer                                         nhjimiiCif1fti.m



cities. The underground water of the said area occupies an extremely
important position for the three cities, and Jinzhou in particular.
Protection and rational-exploitation of underground water of the said
area is an important problem concerning the econornic development
and people's health of Jinzhou, Panjin as well as Jinxi.
14. 2  Dalinghe and Xiaolinghe are two main rivers flowing through the de-
posited fan area of Dalinghe and Xiaolinghe. Due to the fact that all
the industrial waste water and living pollution water of Jinzhou urban
area drains into them, the volatile phenols, petroleum oils and
CODE,,quantity has exceeded the GB3838-88V standards. The soil
erosion at upstream of Dalinghe is great, the organic matter brought
by it causes the river water CODm, exceed the standard (Category V
of GB3838-88) and when waste water of Zincheng Mill enters into
it, the water quality of Dalinghe downstream becomes worst, during
the seven-year dry period from 1985 to 1991 the average amount of
CODm,,reached 143 mg/i and up, exceeding the standard 13. 3 times.
Under its infulence the chemieal oxygon demand in sea area near the
river mouth was as high as 7 mg/l, exceeding the third category sea
water national standard (5 mg/l).
14. 3  40% of underground water supply in fan area of Dalinghe and Xiaol-
inghe comes from Dalinghe and Xiaolinghe. The pollution of the two
rivers has already caused an impact on the fan area underground wa-
ter. In the urban area along the Xiaolinghe river bank (irncluding
Nuerhe) to the west of the fan area and the banks downstream as well
as the irragation area, the underground water in shallow layers is al-
ready polluted by petroleum oils, CODm., etc. Seasonal stop of water
151



supply has emerged in some part of urgan area water source due to
this pollution. Before the solution of Xiaolinghe pollution, it is not
suitable to build new drinking water source in the said areas. Al-
though the broad central area of the fan area and the east area are
threatened by Dalinghe pollution, because the glutinous soil water-
separation layer is relatively thick, the quality of undergrourd water
at prcsent is still good. The suggested new water source is situated in
the central part of the said area, and since the F,Fe excess standard
area (which is harmed by nonartificial pollution, such as geological
conditions, etc) is situated in the downstream of the suggested new
water source and is far away from the deeping-sinking funnel after
the exploitation of the new water source, so the excess standard area
will not cause influence to the newly built water source.
14. 4 Jincheng Mill is the principal pollution source of Jinzhou section of
Dalinghe the pollution load occupies 95% and up of pollution load
drained to the river by Jinzhou City. Having cortrolled the pollution
load of Jinzhou Mill. The pollution load of Jinzhou City to Dalinghe
is basically controlled. After completion of the Jincheng Mill treat-
ment project, the CODcv drainage amount of the Mill will decrease to
20,637 t/a from the present 65,624 t/a, a cut of 68. 55%, so the
CODc, drainage to Dalinghe by the city reduces 66. 5 %; the SS re-
duces to 7,963 t/a from the present 42,386 t/a, a cut of 81. 21%;
the pollution water drainage reduces to 33,185 t/a from the present
65,122 t/a, a cut of 49%, so the drainage of the city to Dalinghe
reduces 31. 2%. The Jincheng Mill treatment project is extaemely
important in Jinzhou City PoLlution Control Plan and The Dalinghe
Pollution Treatment Plan.

recycled DaDer                                   cuhnge aimed mn%inrwnment



14. 5 The Jincheng Mill treatment project starts from the technological re-
form of pulp-making. Changes wastes to values, utilization is con-
ducted in a combined way, water is economised by circulation, and a
two-section reverse-flow washing by double- net pulp- w;ning ma-
chine is adopted, spray-film vacuum evaporator is used, the technol
ogy is advanced and relialle, the predicted results of the project is
thus ensured.
14. 6  After completion of the Jincheng Mill treatment project, the down-
stream water quality of Dalinghe is obviously improved. Computer
imitation results show that during medium water years, the
CODm. average highest quantity in dry period downstream will reduce
48 Y in comparison to that before completion of the project, in medi-
urm water period, it will reduce 5. 7 %o , in full water period it will
reduce 48. 3%. At the same time. the water quality of sea area near
Dalinghe River mouth will improve, in full water period COD"" val-
ue will reach 4. 39 mg/I. reducing 27. 4% compaFed to that before
reform, the underground water quality also will improve. The water
qudity of dry and medium water periods in the suggested water source
will not change much. After completion of Jincheng. Mill treatment
project, the water quality of water source removal and reconstruction
project is guaranteed reliably.
14. 7 The Jincheng Mill treatment project will bring a certain negative im-
pact to the surrounding environment. This is the noise and dust
caused by transportation vehicies during construction and the tail gas-
es produced by artificial charcoals. But the impact is short-term and
153



of smell-scope.
14. 8  The water source removal and reconstruction project is conducted to
meet the requirements in Jinzhou's economical, socicl development
and the rising standard of people's living. After completion of the
project, it will promotc the development of Jinzhou economy. In the
depreciation period of 20 years, the computed economic benefit, af-
ter reduction of expenses for environmental palliation, will at least be
120,000,000 yuar. The living water for the people will rise to
180 1/man * d from the present 16. 2 I/man * d, which directly
raises the quality of people's living. The completion of the project not
only provides to the society employment opportunities, but also,
since it will provids necesscry conditions for social development, it
will indirectly create employment opportunities for the society. In
sum, the water source project has a great economic and social bene-
fit.

yield obvious impact on the surrounding ecological environment.

APPENDIX 1
The Standing Committee of the People's

COMMENTS ON PROJECTS OF BUTILDING
NEW WATERWORKS FOR JINZHOU AND
CONTROLLING WATER POLLUTION CAUSED
BY JINTCHENG PAPER MILL

recvcled oaper               E  i,i,,,   ,m,i, ,, .,



With the growth of the economy and the improvement of the living standards of the
people, the demand for fresh water in urban areas increases continuously. However, due
to industrial pollution, the groundwater in shallow layers are all polluted so severely that
there of the urban water supplies have been forced to stop supplying drinking water s-
sonally. The shortage of water in urban areas is thus more intensified than ever before,
and the economnic development is severely hindered in Jinzhou.
During the convening of the 9th and 10th People's Congresses of the 'Municipality,
the congress representatives put forward 8 proposals on questions concerning water supr'v
and water pollution of Jinzhou. Based on the requirement of these proposals, the munici-
pal government took a series of measures to ease the intensity of the existing problems.
However, we are still facing serious problems of water pollution and water shortage in
our city. It is predicted that by 1995 there will be a shortage of 100,000m'/d of water
and a shortage of 200, 000m3/d by 2000.
According to the report approved by the Committee of Geology and Mineral Reserves
of Liaonrig Province, abundant, high quality groundwater resources exist in th- alluvial
sectors of Daling River and Xiaoling River 15 to 25 km from the urban arear of Jinzhou.
To develop and protect the groundwater resources in the sectors of Daling and Xiaoiing
Rivers is a task of great importance at present and in the nany years to come.
Bseld on the above facts and for the purpose of meeting the demands of the people in
their livelihood of Jinzhou and ensuring the successful operation of our economy, the
Standing Committee of the People's Congress shows concern for and gives support to the
projects of building new water supplies for Jinzhou and controlling water pollution caused
by Jincheng Paper Mill. We agree that the government should make quick endeavours to
solve :he problems of water shortage and water pollutioia, which are the two factors limit-
ing the Living standards and the ewnomic construction of this city.
The Standing ComTnittee of the People's Congress of Jinzhou Municipality
9 October 1992

We welcome and support the projects that the People's Government of Jinzhou plans
to carry out for constructing new water supplies and controlling water pollution caused by
Jincheng Paper Mill.
In recent years, the economy of out city has developed at relatively fast speeds p
however another three water supplies in our city are forced to stop supplying water, thus
gratly impairing the raising of the living standards and the growth of the economy in this
city. Ihe Municipal Political Consultative Committee, on rmany occasions over the past
years, called for attention to problems of industrial pollution and shortage of water, and
submitted to the government propoals urging it to solve the problem of water shortage
and pollution for our city.
In the spirit of responsibility for the, people, the Jinzhou Municipal Government
started preparatory work several years ago for the new water supply project and conducted
investigations on the control of water poUution of Daling and Xiaoling Rivers. The Re-
port on the Study of Model for Groundwarer in Sectors of Daling and Xiaoling Rivers ap-
proved by the Committee of Geology and Mineral Reserves provides reliable scientific
grounds for starting the project of constructing new water supplies.
Government departments have given an overall and detailed consideration to the con-
struction of new water supplies, especially to the problem of protecting the water sources
and planned to solve simultaneously the problem of water pollution of Daling River
caused by Jincheng Paper Mill threatening the future water supply. Hence, the water
quality of the new supply will be protected and more benefits will result from the
project
The projects of building new water supplies and controlling water pollution caused by
Jincheng Paper Mill will be funded with loans from World Band. We are grateful to WB
for its support. We hope that the Jinzhou Municipal Government will make good use of
te funds, ensure the quality of the projects and bring benefits to the people.
Jinzhou Committee, People's Political Consultative Conference of China

A BACKGROUNrD
1 The Alluvial Sectors of Daling and Xiaoling Rivers at Jinzhou Lie in an
Area of 1200km2
In these sectors there are extremely abundand groundwater resources with an ex-
tractable capacity of 1 . 36 million m1 per day. The groundwater in this area is not only a
water supply to meet all the demands of the urban area of Jinzhou, but also functions as
one of the main water sources for another two cities i. e. . Panjin and Jinxi. At present,
Jinzhou draws from this area 1. 02 million m3/d of water for people's livelihood, indu .:rv
and agriculture, while .Jinxi draws 30, 00m3/d for livelihood and industry. To meet the
increasing demand for water, the three above-nentioned cities will have to draw from
those sectors 230, OOOm3/d more. Therefore the groundwater in that area is of extremely
great importance to the three cities, and to Jinzhou above all. The protection of ground-
water resources in that area has a close bearing to the economic development and people's
health of Jinzhou, Panjin and Jinxi.
2 Quality of Groundwater in the Sectors of Daling and Xiaoling Rivers
Assessment was made of the quality of groundwater in the sectors according to Hy-
giene Standards for Dringking Water (GB5749-85). Factors not included in the Stan-
dards were assessed according to water qulity standards for GB3338-88 II surface water
which can be used as drinkable water.. Guroundwater secEors may be divided into the fol-
lowing sections.
2. 1   Fullv Standard Section Where Groundwater Meets All the Standards
for Drinking Water
This section lies in the sector of Daling River and in part of the sector in the upper
reaches of Xiaoling River. Groundwater in this section features good physical properties,
colourlessness, and is colourless tasteless, transparent and free from suspended matters,
with water temperatures ranging from 7 to 12 deg c. Mineralization is less than 1 gil,
chemical type is heavv carbonate, pH7-8. 5. Overall hardness is 200 to 300mg/1.
There is no toxic element like Cu, Pb, Hg, Cr, CN. The content of Fe is between 0. 03
162



and 0. 3 mg/I. Fis less 1 mg/J, As less than 0. 06mg/1, Zn 0. 2 to 0. 3 mg/l. Col-
libacilus content is less than 3/1. This shows that the groundwater in this section fully
meets the standards for drinking water.
T'he Jinzhou Municipal Government plans to build new water supplies within this
section.
2. 2 Single Factor Out-of-bound Section
This section lies to the south of section 1 from the central part of sectors of Daling
and Xiaoling Rivers to Xinzhuangzi, Jianye and Yanjia. Mineralization of water there is
less than Ig/l and the water is of heavy carbonate fresh water type. All specifications of
the water, except Fe content, meet the standards of drinking water. The average Fe con-
tent is 0. 5 to 3 mg/A, exceeding the standard by a factor of 0. 7 to 9.
2.3   Two or More Factors Out- of- bound Section
This section lies in the valley of XiaoLing River and the front areas of sectors of Dal-
ing and Xiaoling Rivers, including the embankment of Xiaoling River, the irrigation area
of Jianye, Dayou, and Baqian. Dayou and Baqian embed heavy corbonate fresh water
with F and Fe exceeding the limits Fe content is 2 to 6 mg/I, one to five times more
than the standards allow. The cause for this is the hydrologic and geological feature of
that area, not human pollution. However, groundwater in the embankment of Xiaoling
River and the Jianye irrigation area is severely polluted, petroliumn content in the water
exceeds the limits and is as high as 0. 6 to 0. 9 mg/l in certain locations.
CODw and SOr2 contents in the groundwater near the river exceeds the limits with
the former ranging between 4 and 5 mg/l and the latter up to 250--450mg/l. The pollu-
tion of the groundwater in the embankment of Xiaoling River and in the Jianye irrigation
area is caused by the supply from the heavily polluted Xiaoling River to groundwater lay-
ers and the irrigation area. The 7 existing water supplies of Jinzhou are all located in this
section. Of them Hepaxinzi, Nanshan and Nuerhe water supplies suffered from seasonal
such severe pollution that they had to stop supplying water. Suifeng and Bozi water sup-
163
recycled caper                                          .hv nid nieinmnmrsii



pies located in the irrigation area of Xiaoling River still have quite good water quality;
but they are under the threat of the sewage supplied to the irrigation area.
3 Pollution of Surface Water in Sectors of Daling and Xiaoling Rivers
40%  of the supply to the groundwater layers in sectors of Daling and XiaoLing
Rivers is from the infiltration of the two rivers. The water quality of the two rivers,
whether good or bad, has a direct impact on the quality of the groundwater in the
sectors.
Water quality survey and measures over past yesrs show that Daling and Xiaoling
Rivers are severely polluted.
Tables 1 and 2 contain the results of surveying the two rivers in the past years.
Hejiaxinzi in Table 1 is the cross section of Xiaoling River before it enters the urban
area. The Tieluqiao and Taoci are two sections of the river passing through the urban
area. Baigu is a crcss section after the river leaves the urban area but before it enters the
irrigation area. Xishulin is a section in the lower reaches of the river. Water quality in
the upper reaches is excellent. Before the river enters the urban area its water quality
reaches the standard GB3838-88 Class I. During the dry season, after Xiaoling River
has passed the urban area, its water is badly polluted with volatile phenol, petrolium par-
ticles, CODm. contents all exceeding the specifications of GB3838-88 Clams V for water
quality. Volatile phenol exceeds Class V spec by a factor of 46, COD, by 2. 4 times and
petrolium particles by 1. 2 times. Special attention should be drawn to the fact that Xiaol-
ing River enters the irrigation area from the lower reaches to the Baigu crcss section and
the supply of the irrigation area to groundwater layers is polluting the shallow groundwa-
ter layers with petrolium, and has become a threat to Suifeng and Bozi water supplies.
Thangjiabao 6cros section listed in Table 2 is located at the top of the sector of Daling
River, which is the source for the horizontal supply to groundwater layers in Daling Riv-
er sector. Xibaqian is the surveyed section of the river after the sewage from Jincheng
Paper Mill flows into the river. The main pollutants in Daling River is CODM, which in-
creases in quantity at Zhangjiabao cross section in the upper reaches with the increase in
river flow. This is caused by the organic matters carried by the water and soil washed into

4 Location of Pollution Sources in Sectors of Daling and Xiaoling Rivers
The pollution sources in the sectors of Daling and Xiaoling Rivers are located in the
urban area of Jinzhou, Jincheng Town and Dalinghe Town. However, pollution sources
are concentrated in Jinzhou urban area, Jincheng Town and Dalinghe Town.
4. 1 Location of Pollution Sources of Xiaoling River and Discharge of Pol-
lutants
Moct of the industrial pollution sources of Xiaoling River are located in the north-
west, west and southeat parts of the urban area. The remaining industrial pollution
sources (including those of neighbour-hood and private enterprises) are scattered here and
there in the city. Sewage from factories and sewage from living quarters run through the
same pipes, ditches and river branches. They enter Xiaoling River at 15 places. In
1990, the urban area discharged 218, 000 m3/d into Xiaoling River, including 81, 000
m3/d from living quarters and 137, 000m3/d from factories. The total urban area dis-
charged 14,190 t/a of COD<>, 755 t/a of petrolium, 20. 27 t/a of volatile phenol. See
Table 3 for details.
There are 15 major pollution sources, of which 9 are most outstanding: Nuerhe Pa-
per Mill, Jinzhou Oil Refinery, Jinzhou Iron Alloy Factory, Jinzhou Chemical Works,
Jinzhou Printing and Dying Mill, Jinzhou Petro-Chemical Factory, Jinzhou Locamotive
Factory, No. 1 Jinzhou Pharmacertical Factory and Jinzhou Chemical Pharmacertical
Factory.

B.. . POLLUTON. CONTROL. PROGRAMME FOR THE PROJECT
- TO PROTECr WATER RESOURCES IN THE SECTORS OF
-DALING AND XIAOLING RIVERS
6 Objectives of the Pollution Control Programme
A systematic control will be exercised over Daling River and its pollution so as to
protect the new water supplies to be contructed and other water resources. Comprehensive
control will be exercised on the pollution of Xiaoling River and the urban area to protect
the unpoUuted water resources from getting poUuted and enable the already polluted water
r^sources to remurn to its clean status. Those are the basic objectives of the progra.nme.
To improve the ecologic environment of the river is also one of the objectives of the pro-
gramne.
6. 1 Qbjective for Controlling Water Quality of Daling River
6. 1. 1 Near-tenn Objective (1995)
Water quality in the lower sections of the river from Jincheng Paper Mill sha  be
improved to a relatively great extent.
6. 1. 2 Mld-term objective (2000)
- Water quality of the river shall be further improved so that in the lower sections of
the river from Jincheng Paper Mill so!able CODm*, COD will reach GB 3838-88 Class
HI standard and that the water supplied by Daling River to the sectors by infiltration will
meet the requirements for protecting Grade 2 water sources.
6. 1. 3 Long-term Objective
Water quality in the lower sections from Jincheng shal reach GB 3838-88 Class III
standard so that Daling River will not only meet the requirements for supplying water to
groundwater layers, but also retain a good ecological status and maritime environment for
recycled paper                      171                  .    sw  li ninwin.nmen



Itself.
6. 2   Objectives for Controlling Water Quality of Xiaoling River
6. 2. 1 Near-terni Objective
Water quality shall be improved notably in the urban sections of the river. In the ir-
rigation season, before the river is diverted into the irrigation channels, water quality
(especially petro content) shall reach GB 3838-88 Class IV standard to prevent or reduce
the pollution of water sources in Suifeng, Bozi and live}ihood water supplies during irriga-
tion.
6. 2. 2 Mid-term Water Quality Objective
Water quality in urban sections shall reach Class TV standard to meet the require-
ments for tourism and recreation in urban areas; in the irrigation season, water quality
shal reach Class III standard before the river is diveted into the irrigation area to protect
water resources in the sectors of Xiaoling River.
6. 2. 3 Long-term Objective
Water quaLity in urban area shall reach Class III standard and meet the requirements
for swimming.
7 Projects for Implementing the Pollution Control Programme
7. 1 Projects for Controlling the Pollution of Daling River
7. 1. 1 Near-term Projects
This is the first-phase project for controlling water pollution caused by Jincheng Pa-
per Mill. The project starts with the renovation of pulping technology and involves the use
of red pulping water to make adhesives, the recoverv of White water in paper naking and
the use of reed chips to make artificial charcoal. After completion of the project, the dis-
172



charge of CODL,from the mill will be reduced by 44,987 t, SS by 3.1,422 t, and sewage
by 30, 000 m3. Thus the city will reduce its discharge of COD into Daling River by
66.5 %, and sewage by 31. 2 %, and the project will play an important role in improving the
water quality of the river, protecting the water supply in Liuduan and improving the
quality of off shore waters. Huge benefits on the environment are expected. The project
will be completed by the end of 199 j. The fund for capital construction totals 56. 55 mil-
lion yuan.
7. .l 2 Mld-terni Project
7.1. 2. 1  This is the second-phase project for controlling water pollution caused by
Jincheng Paper Mill. The project involves the continuation of recovery and use of the red
water and the setting up of a sewage bio-chemical treatment station for the entire mill.
After completion of the project, sewage dicharged from the mill will reach the relevant
standards. The funds required by the project total 40 millon yuan.
7. 1. 2. 2 Projects for controlling water pollution caused by Jirnxan Paper Mill and Jinx-
ian Chernical Fertilizer Factory. After treatment, sewage discharge will reach the rele-
vant stundards. Funds required for these projects are 15 million yuan.
After completion of these mid-term projects, the quantity of COD discharged in Dal-
ing River will be reduced by 17,300 t/a or by 92. 1 Y as compared to the present COD
discharge into Dalirig River by the entire city.
7. 1. 3 Long-term Projects
7. 1. 3. 1 Sewage treatment works project at Daling River Tbwn. This works will be
able to treat 60, 000 In3 of sewage per day and hence rank as Class I sewage treatment
works. The project requires 20 million yuan of funds.
7. l. 3. 2   Project to preserve water and soil in DaLing River reaches. To thoroughly im-
prove the water qualitv of Daling River, it is necessary to preserve water and soil in the
river reaches, -so that the quantity of mud and sand and the organic matters carried by
them can be reduced in the river. The project for preserving water and soil of Daling
reaches calls for the organzation by governments at all levels and the coordination of
173
recycled pDaer                                               I.  nd enqmem,



higher authrities. The preservation of water and soil is a difficult task that takes long term
efforts and persistance. The whole project for preserving water and soil requires a fund of
about 600 million yuan.
7. 2  Project for Controlling the Pollution of Xiaoling River
7. 2. 1 Near-term Project
7. 2. 1. 1 This project is aimed at controlling of the principal pollution snurces, that is,
control of the total discharged amount of pollutants from Jinzhou Oil Refinery, Jinzhou
lIron Alloy Factory, Jinzhou Chermical Factory, Jinzhou Petro- Chemical Factory,
Jinzhou Locamative Maintenance Works and Jinzhou Chekal Pharmaceutical Factory.
These factories will take appropriate measures such as techni4krenovation, comprehen-
sive use of materials and construction of sewage treatmen worksN\o ensure that the dis-
charge of the treated sewage will meet the relevant standards. Contro,of pollution caused
by Jinzhou Iron Alloy Factory using chrome slags for iron making and btinzhou Chemi-
cal Factory sewage will be implemented at the earliest possible date. These projects require
a total fund of 46. 5 million yuan. The results will oe reduction of pollutants like COD,
petroleum, phenol by 2600 t/a, that is, over 25% of the discharge of industrial pollu-
tants of the entire city.
7. 2. 1. 2 Construction of the Oxidation Reservoir
A one million cubic meter Class III Oxidation Reservoir will be constructed to ensure
that the petroleum content in the irrigation water reaches Class IV standard to protect wa-
ter resources at Suifeng, and Bozi. In the dry season (guarantee ratio 90 % ), water will
be kept in the reservoir for 68 hours petroleum content will be reduced by 50% to 70%.
This project requires a fund of 17 million yuan.
7. 2. 2  Mlid-term Project
Between 1996 and 2000, sewage treatment works will be constructed for Jinzhou e-
conomic development zone, hi-tech district. And the northwest Class 2 sewage treatment
works will also be constructed. The one for the EDZ will have a capacity of 30. 000 m3/d
174



while the other two will have a capacity of 50,000 m3/d each. The total funds needed
are 5. rnillion yuan ...bThe completion. of tbcse proects will.ensure, that the water quality of
Xiaoling River in urban area will reach Class IV standard.
7. 2. 3 Long-term Project
7. 2. 3. 1 A Class I sewage treatment works will be constructed with a capacity of
200, 000 mn/d, to treat the livelihood and industrial sewage in the urban area on the left
side of Xiaoling River. The project requires a fund of 67 million yuan.
7. 2. 3. 2 A divertion pipeline will be constructed between the south end of Renmin
Road and the Class 1 sewage treatment works. The pipeline is 8,600 meters long and re-
quires a fund of 18 million yuan.
7. 2. 3. 3 The sewage treatment works in Jinzhou EDZ will be expanded to boast its ca-
pacity of 30,000 ml/d built in mid-term project to 100,000 mO /d to meet the increasing
requirements of the EDZ.
T lhe construction of the above sewage treatment works and the divertion pipeline will
enable the water quality of Xiaoling River to reach Class III standard in all respects.
